[30;1m65 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m42 | [0m[35mCrochet provides the following basic APIs:[0m
[30;1m43 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m44 | [0m[35m* Allow blocking code to call into Twisted and block until results are available[0m
[30;1m45 | [0m[35m  or a timeout is hit, using the ``crochet.wait_for`` decorator.[0m
[30;1m46 | [0m[35m* A lower-level API (``crochet.run_in_reactor``) allows blocking code to run[0m
[30;1m47 | [0m[35m  code "in the background" in the Twisted thread, with the ability to repeatedly[0m
[30;1m48 | [0m[35m  check if it's done.[0m

[30;1m216 | [0m[35m* It is now possible to call ``EventualResult.wait()`` (or functions[0m

[30;1m64 | [0m[35mCrochet provides the following basic APIs:[0m
[30;1m65 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m66 | [0m[35m* Allow blocking code to call into Twisted and block until results are available[0m
[30;1m67 | [0m[35m  or a timeout is hit, using the ``crochet.wait_for`` decorator.[0m
[30;1m68 | [0m[35m* A lower-level API (``crochet.run_in_reactor``) allows blocking code to run[0m
[30;1m69 | [0m[35m  code "in the background" in the Twisted thread, with the ability to repeatedly[0m
[30;1m70 | [0m[35m  check if it's done.[0m
